        <script type="text/javascript">
        function formatCountdown (miliSecond) {
            var day = Math.floor(miliSecond / (3600000 * 24));
            var hour = Math.floor(miliSecond / 3600000 - day * 24);
            var min = Math.floor(miliSecond / 60000 - (day * 24 + hour) * 60);
            var second = Math.floor(miliSecond / 1000 - (day * 24 + hour) * 3600 - min * 60);
            

            
            if (day == 0) {
                return hour + "小时 "
                    + min + "分 "
                    + second + "秒";
            } else {
                return day + "天 "
                    + hour + "小时 "
                    + min + "分 ";
            }
        }
        
        function leadingZero (value) {
            if (value/10 < 1) {
                return "0" + value;
            }
            return value;
        }

        if(window.P && window.P.AUI_BUILD_DATE) {
            P.when('A', 'jQuery', 'ready').execute(function (A, $) {
                A.interval(function() {
                    var currentTime = new Date().getTime();
                    $(".ags_deal_action_container").each(function() {
                        var actionButton = $(this).find(".deal_item_button_input");
                        var startTime = $(this).find("input[name=startTime]").val();
                        var endTime = $(this).find("input[name=endTime]").val();
                        var timerLabel = $(this).find(".ags_deal_timer_label");
                        var timerCountdown = $(this).find(".ags_deal_timer_countdown");
                        if (typeof timerLabel === "undefined" ||
                            typeof timerCountdown === "undefined" ||
                            typeof startTime === "undefined" ||
                            typeof endTime === "undefined") {
                            return;
                        } else if (startTime > currentTime) {
                            timerLabel.html("距离开始 ");
                            var remainingTime = startTime - currentTime;
                            timerCountdown.html(formatCountdown(remainingTime));
                            $(actionButton).attr("disabled", "disabled");
                        } else if (currentTime > endTime) {
                            timerLabel.html("活动结束");
                            timerCountdown.html("");
                            $(actionButton).attr("disabled", "disabled");
                        } else {
                            timerLabel.html("剩余时间 ");
                            var remainingTime = endTime - currentTime;
                            var date = new Date(remainingTime);
                            timerCountdown.html(formatCountdown(remainingTime));
                            $(actionButton).removeAttr("disabled");
                        }
                    })
                }, 1000);
            });

<script type="text/javascript">

function CNRightTrailBanner($){

  var status=0;

  var bannerBackgroundColorArray = 
  ['#D8AE5A',
   '#C6C6C2',
   '#9CC9AB',
   '#5BABC3',
   '#CEC55C',
   '#89D793']; 
  
  function Render(){
      $.ajax({
          type: 'POST',
          url: '/gp/cn-right-trail-banner/ajaxGetRightTrailBannerContentHtmlV2.html/462-8128257-5838428',
          data: {"callMethod":"getPromotionsFromOACS","promotionFilter":"%5B%22A2ERXUNM5V6OO5%22%2C%22A244O14TINE2H4%22%2C%22A1ETZ07YQZY88F%22%2C%22A16BL2UYBZ0O36%22%2C%22ALX0WJAW2JCAA%22%2C%22A38SGHUQ2XJYF3%22%2C%22A35MTTFCKJ9E7%22%2C%22A1ETZ07YQZY88F%22%2C%22A16BL2UYBZ0O36%22%2C%22ALX0WJAW2JCAA%22%2C%22A1ETZ07YQZY88F%22%2C%22A440WI8T3KOAO%22%2C%22A3F3AQQ33U02B5%22%5D","rId":"52JX2PQC4DK5BPD5MQ43","redirectUrl":"#?pf_rd_p=90d949ce-082b-4ead-9337-d54e78eef216&pf_rd_s=desktop-sidekick-2&pf_rd_t=36701&pf_rd_i=desktop&pf_rd_m=A1AJ19PSB66TGU&pf_rd_r=52JX2PQC4DK5BPD5MQ43&pf_rd_r=52JX2PQC4DK5BPD5MQ43&pf_rd_p=90d949ce-082b-4ead-9337-d54e78eef216"},
          dataType: 'text',
          cache: false,
          contentType: 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded; charset=utf-8',
          timeout: 40000,
          success: function(data) {
              data = eval('('+data+')');
              var contentHtml = data.contentHtml;
	              
              for (var i=0;i<6;i++){
                $('.cn-right-trail-banner .cn-right-trail-banner-holder').append(contentHtml[i]);
                $('.cn-right-trail-banner .cn-right-trail-banner-holder .bannerBlock:eq('+i+')').css({'background-color':bannerBackgroundColorArray[i]});
                //$('.cn-right-trail-banner .cn-right-trail-banner-holder .bannerBlock:eq('+i+') .bannerBlockBackground .bannerLeftContent .glName').css({'color':bannerBackgroundColorArray[i]});
              }
              //Bind hover event
             $('.cn-right-trail-banner .cn-right-trail-banner-holder .bannerBlock').hover(
                function(){
                    $(this).find('.promotionUrl').css({'color':'#E47911'});
                },
                function(){
                    $(this).find('.promotionUrl').css({'color':'#767676'});
                }
            );
          }
      });
  }
  
  Render();
}
 
if (typeof amznJQ !== 'undefined'){
  amznJQ.available('jQuery',function(){
      var $ = jQuery;
      amznJQ.available('cf').execute(function(){
          CNRightTrailBanner($);
      });
  });
} else if (typeof P !== 'undefined') {
  P.when('A').execute(function(a) {
      var $ = a.$, jQuery = a.$;
      P.when('cf').execute(function(){
          CNRightTrailBanner($);
      });
  });
}

function cnGwiterjs(zdurl, zdparams, pdurl, pdparams, bookurl, bookparams, bsurl, bsparams){
    function getAjaxContent($){
        var firstSlot  = $('#gw-iter-content-1');
        var secondSlot = $('#gw-iter-content-2');
        var thirdSlot  = $('#gw-iter-content-3');
        var fourthSlot = $('#gw-iter-content-4');
        var count = 0;
        // First Slot 
        $.ajax({
            type: 'POST',
            url: zdurl,
            data: zdparams,
            dataType: 'text',
            cache: true,
            contentType: 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded; charset=utf-8',
            timeout: 40000,
            success: function(data) {
                data=eval('('+data+')');
                asincontent = data.asinContentList;
                firstSlot.append(asincontent);
                count++;
                if (count==4) {
                    $(".gw-iter-title-href").hover(
                        function(){
                            $(this).children('.gw-iter-title-black').css('color','#FF8C00');
                        },
                        function(){
                            $(this).children('.gw-iter-title-black').css('color','#333333');
                        }
                    );
                    $(window).resize(gwIterResize);
                    gwIterResize();
                }
            }
        });
        
        // Second Slot

            type: 'POST',

            data: pdparams,
            dataType: 'text',
            cache: true,

        // Third Slot

function gwIterResize(){
        if (typeof BtechRSA !== 'undefined') BtechRSA.bunkBedResize();
    var language = 'zh';
    var enOffset = 0;
    if (language =='en') {
        enOffset = 75;
    }
    P.when('A').execute(function(A){
        var $ = A.$;
        var screenwidth = $(window).width();
        var itercontent = $('#' + "desktop-1");
        var containerWidth;
        var lesswidth = 0;
        
        if (screenwidth>=1880){
            lesswidth=enOffset;
            itercontent.css({'margin-left':enOffset+'px'});
        } else if (screenwidth<1233) {
            lesswidth=enOffset;
            itercontent.css({'margin-left':'0'});
        } else if (screenwidth>=1500){
            lesswidth=(1880-screenwidth)/2+enOffset;
            itercontent.css({'margin-left':lesswidth+'px'});
        } else if (screenwidth>=1233){
            lesswidth=190+enOffset;
            itercontent.css({'margin-left':lesswidth+'px'});
        }
        var containerWidth = document.getElementById('btfContent').offsetWidth-40-lesswidth;
        if(containerWidth==0) return;
        if(containerWidth<660) containerWidth=660;
        if (containerWidth < 526){
        } else if (containerWidth < 789 && containerWidth >=526){
            iterAlterDisplay(2,containerWidth);
        } else if (containerWidth < 1052 && containerWidth >= 789){
            iterAlterDisplay(3,containerWidth);
        } else if (containerWidth >= 1035) {
            iterAlterDisplay(4,containerWidth);
        }
    });
            
        
    document.getElementById('gw-iter-block').style.display='inline';
    }
    function iterAlterDisplay(MidNumber,CenterWidth){
        document.getElementById('gw-iter-center').style.width               = CenterWidth+"px";
        for (var i=4;i>=MidNumber+1;i--){
            document.getElementById('gw-iter-content-'+i).style.display     = 'none';
            document.getElementById('gw-iter-division-'+i).style.display    = 'none';
        }
        for (var i=1;i<=MidNumber;i++){
            var content    = document.getElementById('gw-iter-content-'+i);
            var header     = document.getElementById('gw-iter-header-'+i);
            var title      = document.getElementById('gw-iter-title-'+i);
            var titleFont  = document.getElementById('gw-iter-title-font-'+i);
            var contentAdd = (CenterWidth-MidNumber*264)/MidNumber;
            if (content && content.style && header && header.style){
                content.style.width        = (CenterWidth-5)/MidNumber+"px";
                header.style.width         = content.style.width;
                title.style.width          = content.style.width;
                titleFont.style.marginLeft = 10+contentAdd*0.3+"px";
                var img                    = document.getElementById('gw-iter-img-'+i);
                if (img){
                    var detail              = document.getElementById('gw-iter-detail-'+i);
                    detail.style.marginLeft = 10+contentAdd*0.3+"px";
                    img.style.right         = contentAdd*0.3+"px";
                    detail.style.width      = 108+contentAdd*0.4+"px";
                }
                content.style.display = 'inline';
            }
            if (i>=2) document.getElementById('gw-iter-division-'+i).style.display='inline';
        }
    }

<script type="text/javascript">
function getdyfloors9ImgWidth(width,height,standardw,standardh,minwidth){
                var ans=standardw; 
                if (width<=standardw && height<=standardh)
                    ans=width;
                else if (width>standardw && height<=standardh)
                    ans=standardw;
                else if (width<=standardw && height>standardh)
                    ans=width*standardh/height;
                else if (width>standardw && height>standardh){
                    if (standardw/width*height<=standardh)
                        ans=standardw;
                    else
                        ans=width*standardh/height;
                }
                if (ans<minwidth)
                    return minwidth;
                else 
                    return ans;
            }
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
var AGSgfloorstatus = 0;
function AGScheck($){
    var windowtop  = $(window).scrollTop();
    var windowfoot = windowtop+$(window).height();
    var preheight  = 400;
    var thisfloor  = $('#AGSgfloor');
    var floorheight= 470;
    var floortop   = thisfloor.offset().top;
    var floorfoot  = floortop+floorheight;
    if ((floortop>windowfoot && floortop<windowfoot+preheight) 
        || (floorfoot<windowtop && floorfoot+preheight>windowtop) 
        || (floorfoot>windowtop && floortop<windowfoot)){
            AGSgfloorstatus = 1;
            AGSRender($);
            $(window).resize(function(){
                AGSresize($, thisfloor,0);
            });
    }
}
function AGSresize($,thisfloor,status){
    var screenwidth = thisfloor.width();
    if (screenwidth>=1470){
        alterfloor(7);
    } else if (screenwidth<1470 && screenwidth>=1260){
        changesize(1470,7);
    } else if (screenwidth<1260 && screenwidth>=1080) {
        changesize(1260,6);
    } else if (screenwidth<1080 && screenwidth>=1040) {
        alterfloor(5);
    } else if (screenwidth<1040 && screenwidth>=900) {
        changesize(1040,5);
    } else if (screenwidth<900 && screenwidth>=840) {
        alterfloor(4);
    } else if (screenwidth<840 && screenwidth>=720) {
        changesize(840,4);
    } else if (screenwidth<720) {
        alterfloor(3);
    }
    function alterfloor(showNumber){
        var floorContent = thisfloor.find('.gfloorContent');
        var header = thisfloor.find('.gfloorHeader');
        var firstline = thisfloor.find('.gfloor-first-line');
        var secondline = thisfloor.find('.gfloor-second-line');
        hidecell(firstline,showNumber);
        hidecell(secondline,showNumber);
        floorContent.width(210*showNumber);
        header.width(210*showNumber);
        thisfloor.find('.gfloorfbrand').css({'margin-top':30});
        thisfloor.find('.gfloorsbrand').css({'margin-top':30});
        firstline.width(210*showNumber);firstline.height(210);
        secondline.width(210*showNumber);secondline.height(210);
        thisfloor.find('.gfloorcell').width(210);
        thisfloor.find('.gfloorcell').height(210);
        thisfloor.find('.gfloorbigprice').css({'font-size':42});
        thisfloor.find('.gfnewContent').css({'font-size':24});
        thisfloor.find('.gfcontentbuy').css({'bottom':40});
    }
    
    function changesize(maxWdith,showNumber){
        var floorContent = thisfloor.find('.gfloorContent');
        var header = thisfloor.find('.gfloorHeader');
        var losswidth = maxWdith - screenwidth;
        var perlosswidth = losswidth / showNumber;
        var firstline = thisfloor.find('.gfloor-first-line');
        var secondline = thisfloor.find('.gfloor-second-line');
        hidecell(firstline,showNumber);
        hidecell(secondline,showNumber);
        var allwidth = 210*showNumber-losswidth
        floorContent.width(allwidth);
        header.width(allwidth);
        thisfloor.find('.gfloorfbrand').css({'margin-top':30-perlosswidth/3});
        thisfloor.find('.gfloorsbrand').css({'margin-top':30-perlosswidth/3});
        firstline.width(allwidth+1);firstline.height(210-perlosswidth);
        secondline.width(allwidth+1);secondline.height(210-perlosswidth);
        thisfloor.find('.gfloorcell').width(210-perlosswidth);
        thisfloor.find('.gfloorcell').height(210-perlosswidth);
        thisfloor.find('.gfloorbigprice').css({'font-size':42-perlosswidth/3});
        thisfloor.find('.gfnewContent').css({'font-size':24-perlosswidth/10});
        thisfloor.find('.gfcontentbuy').css({'bottom':40-perlosswidth/3});
    }
    function hideType(fline, lossNum, typename){
        var hideCell = fline.find(typename);
        var hideSize = hideCell.length;
        if (lossNum>0){
            for (var i=hideSize-1;i>=0;i--){
                hideCell[i].style.display='none';
                lossNum--;
                if (lossNum<=0){
                    for (var j=i-1;j>=0;j--)
                        hideCell[j].style.display='block';
                    break;
                }
            }
        } else {
            for (var j=0;j<hideSize;j++)
                hideCell[j].style.display='block';
        }
        return lossNum;
    }
    function hidecell(fline,showNumber){
        var lossNumber = 7-showNumber;
        lossNumber = hideType(fline,lossNumber, '.gfloorhotword');
        lossNumber = hideType(fline,lossNumber, '.gfloorasinbs');
        
        var promotionCell = fline.find('.gfloorpromotiontext');
        var asinCell = fline.find('.gfloorasincell');
        var promotionSize = promotionCell.length;
        var asinSize = asinCell.length;
        
        if (lossNumber>0){
            var lossPACell = asinSize*2-(showNumber-1);
            if (lossPACell<0)
                lossPACell = 0;
            var lossPair = Math.floor(lossPACell/2);
            for (var i=0;i<lossPair;i++){
                promotionCell[promotionSize-i-1] && promotionCell[promotionSize-i-1].style && (promotionCell[promotionSize-i-1].style.display = 'none');
                asinCell[asinSize-i-1] && asinCell[asinSize-i-1].style && (asinCell[asinSize-i-1].style.display = 'none');
            }
            if (lossPACell%2==1){
                asinCell[asinSize-lossPair-1] && asinCell[asinSize-lossPair-1].style && (asinCell[asinSize-lossPair-1].style.display='none');
                promotionCell[asinSize-lossPair-1] && promotionCell[asinSize-lossPair-1].style && (promotionCell[asinSize-lossPair-1].style.display='block');
            } else {
                asinCell[asinSize-lossPair-1] && asinCell[asinSize-lossPair-1].style && (asinCell[asinSize-lossPair-1].style.display='block');
                promotionCell[asinSize-lossPair-1] && promotionCell[asinSize-lossPair-1].style && (promotionCell[asinSize-lossPair-1].style.display='block');
            }
            for (var i=0;i<asinSize-lossPair-1;i++){
                asinCell[i] && asinCell[i].style && (asinCell[i].style.display='block');
                promotionCell[i] && promotionCell[i].style && (promotionCell[i].style.display='block');
            }
        } else {
            for (var j=0;j<asinSize;j++){
                asinCell[j] && asinCell[j].style && (asinCell[j].style.display='block');
                promotionCell[j] && promotionCell[j].style && (promotionCell[j].style.display='block');
            }
        }
        
        
    }
}
function AGSRender($){
    $.ajax({
        type: 'POST',
        url: '/gp/grid-floor-widget/ajaxGetGridContent.html/462-8128257-5838428',
        data: {"floorType":"AGS","rId":"52JX2PQC4DK5BPD5MQ43","arrow":"https://images-cn.ssl-images-amazon.com/images/G/28/gwfloor/static/images/arrow_small_white._CB304609528_.png","redirectUrl":"#?pf_rd_p=de9bf570-0292-48c6-afed-1492835470c4&pf_rd_s=desktop-4&pf_rd_t=36701&pf_rd_i=desktop&pf_rd_m=A1AJ19PSB66TGU&pf_rd_r=52JX2PQC4DK5BPD5MQ43&pf_rd_r=52JX2PQC4DK5BPD5MQ43&pf_rd_p=de9bf570-0292-48c6-afed-1492835470c4"},

            AGSresize($, $('#AGSgfloor'),1);
        }
    });
}

<script type="text/javascript">
var SOFTLINEgfloorstatus = 0;
function SOFTLINEcheck($){
    var windowtop  = $(window).scrollTop();
    var windowfoot = windowtop+$(window).height();
    var preheight  = 400;
    var thisfloor  = $('#SOFTLINEgfloor');
    var floorheight= 470;
    var floortop   = thisfloor.offset().top;
    var floorfoot  = floortop+floorheight;
    if ((floortop>windowfoot && floortop<windowfoot+preheight) 
        || (floorfoot<windowtop && floorfoot+preheight>windowtop) 
        || (floorfoot>windowtop && floortop<windowfoot)){
            SOFTLINEgfloorstatus = 1;
            SOFTLINERender($);
            $(window).resize(function(){
                SOFTLINEresize($, thisfloor,0);
            });
    }
}
function SOFTLINEresize($,thisfloor,status){
    var screenwidth = thisfloor.width();
    if (screenwidth>=1470){
        alterfloor(7);
    } else if (screenwidth<1470 && screenwidth>=1260){
        changesize(1470,7);
    } else if (screenwidth<1260 && screenwidth>=1080) {
        changesize(1260,6);
    } else if (screenwidth<1080 && screenwidth>=1040) {
        alterfloor(5);
    } else if (screenwidth<1040 && screenwidth>=900) {
        changesize(1040,5);
    } else if (screenwidth<900 && screenwidth>=840) {
        alterfloor(4);
    } else if (screenwidth<840 && screenwidth>=720) {
        changesize(840,4);
    } else if (screenwidth<720) {
        alterfloor(3);
    }
    function alterfloor(showNumber){
        var floorContent = thisfloor.find('.gfloorContent');
        var header = thisfloor.find('.gfloorHeader');
        var firstline = thisfloor.find('.gfloor-first-line');
        var secondline = thisfloor.find('.gfloor-second-line');
        hidecell(firstline,showNumber);
        hidecell(secondline,showNumber);
        floorContent.width(210*showNumber);
        header.width(210*showNumber);
        thisfloor.find('.gfloorfbrand').css({'margin-top':30});
        thisfloor.find('.gfloorsbrand').css({'margin-top':30});
        firstline.width(210*showNumber);firstline.height(210);
        secondline.width(210*showNumber);secondline.height(210);
        thisfloor.find('.gfloorcell').width(210);
        thisfloor.find('.gfloorcell').height(210);
        thisfloor.find('.gfloorbigprice').css({'font-size':42});
        thisfloor.find('.gfnewContent').css({'font-size':24});
        thisfloor.find('.gfcontentbuy').css({'bottom':40});
    }
    
    function changesize(maxWdith,showNumber){
        var floorContent = thisfloor.find('.gfloorContent');
        var header = thisfloor.find('.gfloorHeader');
        var losswidth = maxWdith - screenwidth;
        var perlosswidth = losswidth / showNumber;
        var firstline = thisfloor.find('.gfloor-first-line');
        var secondline = thisfloor.find('.gfloor-second-line');
        hidecell(firstline,showNumber);
        hidecell(secondline,showNumber);
        var allwidth = 210*showNumber-losswidth
        floorContent.width(allwidth);
        header.width(allwidth);
        thisfloor.find('.gfloorfbrand').css({'margin-top':30-perlosswidth/3});
        thisfloor.find('.gfloorsbrand').css({'margin-top':30-perlosswidth/3});
        firstline.width(allwidth+1);firstline.height(210-perlosswidth);
        secondline.width(allwidth+1);secondline.height(210-perlosswidth);
        thisfloor.find('.gfloorcell').width(210-perlosswidth);
        thisfloor.find('.gfloorcell').height(210-perlosswidth);
        thisfloor.find('.gfloorbigprice').css({'font-size':42-perlosswidth/3});
        thisfloor.find('.gfnewContent').css({'font-size':24-perlosswidth/10});
        thisfloor.find('.gfcontentbuy').css({'bottom':40-perlosswidth/3});
    }
    function hideType(fline, lossNum, typename){
        var hideCell = fline.find(typename);
        var hideSize = hideCell.length;
        if (lossNum>0){
            for (var i=hideSize-1;i>=0;i--){
                hideCell[i].style.display='none';
                lossNum--;
                if (lossNum<=0){
                    for (var j=i-1;j>=0;j--)
                        hideCell[j].style.display='block';
                    break;
                }
            }
        } else {
            for (var j=0;j<hideSize;j++)
                hideCell[j].style.display='block';
        }
        return lossNum;
    }
    function hidecell(fline,showNumber){
        var lossNumber = 7-showNumber;
        lossNumber = hideType(fline,lossNumber, '.gfloorhotword');
        lossNumber = hideType(fline,lossNumber, '.gfloorasinbs');
        
        var promotionCell = fline.find('.gfloorpromotiontext');
        var asinCell = fline.find('.gfloorasincell');
        var promotionSize = promotionCell.length;
        var asinSize = asinCell.length;
        
        if (lossNumber>0){
            var lossPACell = asinSize*2-(showNumber-1);
            if (lossPACell<0)
                lossPACell = 0;
            var lossPair = Math.floor(lossPACell/2);
            for (var i=0;i<lossPair;i++){
                promotionCell[promotionSize-i-1] && promotionCell[promotionSize-i-1].style && (promotionCell[promotionSize-i-1].style.display = 'none');
                asinCell[asinSize-i-1] && asinCell[asinSize-i-1].style && (asinCell[asinSize-i-1].style.display = 'none');
            }
            if (lossPACell%2==1){
                asinCell[asinSize-lossPair-1] && asinCell[asinSize-lossPair-1].style && (asinCell[asinSize-lossPair-1].style.display='none');
                promotionCell[asinSize-lossPair-1] && promotionCell[asinSize-lossPair-1].style && (promotionCell[asinSize-lossPair-1].style.display='block');
            } else {
                asinCell[asinSize-lossPair-1] && asinCell[asinSize-lossPair-1].style && (asinCell[asinSize-lossPair-1].style.display='block');
                promotionCell[asinSize-lossPair-1] && promotionCell[asinSize-lossPair-1].style && (promotionCell[asinSize-lossPair-1].style.display='block');
            }
            for (var i=0;i<asinSize-lossPair-1;i++){
                asinCell[i] && asinCell[i].style && (asinCell[i].style.display='block');
                promotionCell[i] && promotionCell[i].style && (promotionCell[i].style.display='block');
            }
        } else {
            for (var j=0;j<asinSize;j++){
                asinCell[j] && asinCell[j].style && (asinCell[j].style.display='block');
                promotionCell[j] && promotionCell[j].style && (promotionCell[j].style.display='block');
            }
        }
        
        
    }
}
function SOFTLINERender($){
    $.ajax({
        type: 'POST',
        url: '/gp/grid-floor-widget/ajaxGetGridContent.html/462-8128257-5838428',
        data: {"floorType":"SOFTLINE","rId":"52JX2PQC4DK5BPD5MQ43","arrow":"https://images-cn.ssl-images-amazon.com/images/G/28/gwfloor/static/images/arrow_small_white._CB304609528_.png","redirectUrl":"#?pf_rd_p=c85667de-afcd-4b0d-a883-1fe71ab79894&pf_rd_s=desktop-6&pf_rd_t=36701&pf_rd_i=desktop&pf_rd_m=A1AJ19PSB66TGU&pf_rd_r=52JX2PQC4DK5BPD5MQ43&pf_rd_r=52JX2PQC4DK5BPD5MQ43&pf_rd_p=c85667de-afcd-4b0d-a883-1fe71ab79894"},
        dataType: 'text',
        cache: false,
        contentType: 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded; charset=utf-8',
        timeout: 40000,
        success: function(data) {
            data = eval('('+data+')');
            var contentHtml = data.contentHtml;
            $('#SOFTLINEgfloorcontent').append(contentHtml);
            $('#SOFTLINEgfloorcontent .gfloorasincelldiv').css({'opacity':0.85});
            $('#SOFTLINEgfloorcontent .gfloorblockcell').css({'opacity':0.8});
            $('#SOFTLINEgfloorcontent .gfloorasincelldiv').hover(
                function(){
                    $(this).stop(true,true).animate({opacity:0.95},200);
                },
                function(){
                    $(this).stop(true,true).animate({opacity:0.85},200);
                }
            );
            $('#SOFTLINEgfloorcontent .gfloorblockcell').hover(
                function(){
                    $(this).stop(true,true).animate({opacity:0.9},200);
                },
                function(){
                    $(this).stop(true,true).animate({opacity:0.8},200);
                }
            );
            $('#SOFTLINEgfloorcontent .gfloorpromotiontext').hover(
                function(){
                    $(this).find('.gfcontentbspan').css({'color':'#E47911'});
                },
                function(){
                    $(this).find('.gfcontentbspan').css({'color':'#767676'});
                }
            );
            $('#SOFTLINEgfloorcontent .gfloorbstext').hover(
                function(){
                    $(this).find('.gfcontentbspan').css({'color':'#E47911'});
                },
                function(){
                    $(this).find('.gfcontentbspan').css({'color':'#767676'});
                }
            );
            SOFTLINEresize($, $('#SOFTLINEgfloor'),1);
        }
    });
}

    amznJQ.available('jQuery',function(){

        SOFTLINEcheck($);
        $(window).scroll(function(){

                SOFTLINEcheck($);
            }
        });
    });

            }
        });
    });
}

<script type="text/javascript">
var CEgfloorstatus = 0;
function CEcheck($){
    var windowtop  = $(window).scrollTop();
    var windowfoot = windowtop+$(window).height();
    var preheight  = 400;
    var thisfloor  = $('#CEgfloor');
    var floorheight= 470;
    var floortop   = thisfloor.offset().top;
    var floorfoot  = floortop+floorheight;
    if ((floortop>windowfoot && floortop<windowfoot+preheight) 
        || (floorfoot<windowtop && floorfoot+preheight>windowtop) 
        || (floorfoot>windowtop && floortop<windowfoot)){
            CEgfloorstatus = 1;
            CERender($);
            $(window).resize(function(){
                CEresize($, thisfloor,0);
            });
    }
}
function CEresize($,thisfloor,status){
    var screenwidth = thisfloor.width();
    if (screenwidth>=1470){
        alterfloor(7);
    } else if (screenwidth<1470 && screenwidth>=1260){
        changesize(1470,7);
    } else if (screenwidth<1260 && screenwidth>=1080) {
        changesize(1260,6);
    } else if (screenwidth<1080 && screenwidth>=1040) {
        alterfloor(5);
    } else if (screenwidth<1040 && screenwidth>=900) {
        changesize(1040,5);
    } else if (screenwidth<900 && screenwidth>=840) {
        alterfloor(4);
    } else if (screenwidth<840 && screenwidth>=720) {
        changesize(840,4);
    } else if (screenwidth<720) {
        alterfloor(3);
    }
    function alterfloor(showNumber){
        var floorContent = thisfloor.find('.gfloorContent');
        var header = thisfloor.find('.gfloorHeader');
        var firstline = thisfloor.find('.gfloor-first-line');
        var secondline = thisfloor.find('.gfloor-second-line');
        hidecell(firstline,showNumber);
        hidecell(secondline,showNumber);
        floorContent.width(210*showNumber);
        header.width(210*showNumber);
        thisfloor.find('.gfloorfbrand').css({'margin-top':30});
        thisfloor.find('.gfloorsbrand').css({'margin-top':30});
        firstline.width(210*showNumber);firstline.height(210);
        secondline.width(210*showNumber);secondline.height(210);
        thisfloor.find('.gfloorcell').width(210);
        thisfloor.find('.gfloorcell').height(210);
        thisfloor.find('.gfloorbigprice').css({'font-size':42});
        thisfloor.find('.gfnewContent').css({'font-size':24});
        thisfloor.find('.gfcontentbuy').css({'bottom':40});
    }
    
    function changesize(maxWdith,showNumber){
        var floorContent = thisfloor.find('.gfloorContent');
        var header = thisfloor.find('.gfloorHeader');
        var losswidth = maxWdith - screenwidth;
        var perlosswidth = losswidth / showNumber;
        var firstline = thisfloor.find('.gfloor-first-line');
        var secondline = thisfloor.find('.gfloor-second-line');
        hidecell(firstline,showNumber);
        hidecell(secondline,showNumber);
        var allwidth = 210*showNumber-losswidth
        floorContent.width(allwidth);
        header.width(allwidth);
        thisfloor.find('.gfloorfbrand').css({'margin-top':30-perlosswidth/3});
        thisfloor.find('.gfloorsbrand').css({'margin-top':30-perlosswidth/3});
        firstline.width(allwidth+1);firstline.height(210-perlosswidth);
        secondline.width(allwidth+1);secondline.height(210-perlosswidth);
        thisfloor.find('.gfloorcell').width(210-perlosswidth);
        thisfloor.find('.gfloorcell').height(210-perlosswidth);
        thisfloor.find('.gfloorbigprice').css({'font-size':42-perlosswidth/3});
        thisfloor.find('.gfnewContent').css({'font-size':24-perlosswidth/10});
        thisfloor.find('.gfcontentbuy').css({'bottom':40-perlosswidth/3});
    }
    function hideType(fline, lossNum, typename){
        var hideCell = fline.find(typename);
        var hideSize = hideCell.length;
        if (lossNum>0){
            for (var i=hideSize-1;i>=0;i--){
                hideCell[i].style.display='none';
                lossNum--;
                if (lossNum<=0){
                    for (var j=i-1;j>=0;j--)
                        hideCell[j].style.display='block';
                    break;
                }
            }
        } else {
            for (var j=0;j<hideSize;j++)
                hideCell[j].style.display='block';
        }
        return lossNum;
    }
    function hidecell(fline,showNumber){
        var lossNumber = 7-showNumber;
        lossNumber = hideType(fline,lossNumber, '.gfloorhotword');
        lossNumber = hideType(fline,lossNumber, '.gfloorasinbs');
        
        var promotionCell = fline.find('.gfloorpromotiontext');
        var asinCell = fline.find('.gfloorasincell');
        var promotionSize = promotionCell.length;
        var asinSize = asinCell.length;
        
        if (lossNumber>0){
            var lossPACell = asinSize*2-(showNumber-1);
            if (lossPACell<0)
                lossPACell = 0;
            var lossPair = Math.floor(lossPACell/2);
            for (var i=0;i<lossPair;i++){
                promotionCell[promotionSize-i-1] && promotionCell[promotionSize-i-1].style && (promotionCell[promotionSize-i-1].style.display = 'none');
                asinCell[asinSize-i-1] && asinCell[asinSize-i-1].style && (asinCell[asinSize-i-1].style.display = 'none');
            }
            if (lossPACell%2==1){
                asinCell[asinSize-lossPair-1] && asinCell[asinSize-lossPair-1].style && (asinCell[asinSize-lossPair-1].style.display='none');
                promotionCell[asinSize-lossPair-1] && promotionCell[asinSize-lossPair-1].style && (promotionCell[asinSize-lossPair-1].style.display='block');
            } else {
                asinCell[asinSize-lossPair-1] && asinCell[asinSize-lossPair-1].style && (asinCell[asinSize-lossPair-1].style.display='block');
                promotionCell[asinSize-lossPair-1] && promotionCell[asinSize-lossPair-1].style && (promotionCell[asinSize-lossPair-1].style.display='block');
            }
            for (var i=0;i<asinSize-lossPair-1;i++){
                asinCell[i] && asinCell[i].style && (asinCell[i].style.display='block');
                promotionCell[i] && promotionCell[i].style && (promotionCell[i].style.display='block');
            }
        } else {
            for (var j=0;j<asinSize;j++){
                asinCell[j] && asinCell[j].style && (asinCell[j].style.display='block');
                promotionCell[j] && promotionCell[j].style && (promotionCell[j].style.display='block');
            }
        }
        
        
    }
}

<script type="text/javascript">
var BMVDgfloorstatus = 0;
function BMVDcheck($){
    var windowtop  = $(window).scrollTop();
    var windowfoot = windowtop+$(window).height();
    var preheight  = 400;
    var thisfloor  = $('#BMVDgfloor');
    var floorheight= 470;
    var floortop   = thisfloor.offset().top;
    var floorfoot  = floortop+floorheight;
    if ((floortop>windowfoot && floortop<windowfoot+preheight) 
        || (floorfoot<windowtop && floorfoot+preheight>windowtop) 
        || (floorfoot>windowtop && floortop<windowfoot)){
            BMVDgfloorstatus = 1;
            BMVDRender($);
            $(window).resize(function(){
                BMVDresize($, thisfloor,0);
            });
    }
}
function BMVDresize($,thisfloor,status){
    var screenwidth = thisfloor.width();
    if (screenwidth>=1470){
        alterfloor(7);
    } else if (screenwidth<1470 && screenwidth>=1260){
        changesize(1470,7);
    } else if (screenwidth<1260 && screenwidth>=1080) {
        changesize(1260,6);
    } else if (screenwidth<1080 && screenwidth>=1040) {
        alterfloor(5);
    } else if (screenwidth<1040 && screenwidth>=900) {
        changesize(1040,5);
    } else if (screenwidth<900 && screenwidth>=840) {
        alterfloor(4);
    } else if (screenwidth<840 && screenwidth>=720) {
        changesize(840,4);
    } else if (screenwidth<720) {
        alterfloor(3);
    }
    function alterfloor(showNumber){
        var floorContent = thisfloor.find('.gfloorContent');
        var header = thisfloor.find('.gfloorHeader');
        var firstline = thisfloor.find('.gfloor-first-line');
        var secondline = thisfloor.find('.gfloor-second-line');
        hidecell(firstline,showNumber);
        hidecell(secondline,showNumber);
        floorContent.width(210*showNumber);
        header.width(210*showNumber);
        thisfloor.find('.gfloorfbrand').css({'margin-top':30});
        thisfloor.find('.gfloorsbrand').css({'margin-top':30});
        firstline.width(210*showNumber);firstline.height(210);
        secondline.width(210*showNumber);secondline.height(210);
        thisfloor.find('.gfloorcell').width(210);
        thisfloor.find('.gfloorcell').height(210);
        thisfloor.find('.gfloorbigprice').css({'font-size':42});
        thisfloor.find('.gfnewContent').css({'font-size':24});
        thisfloor.find('.gfcontentbuy').css({'bottom':40});
    }
    
    function changesize(maxWdith,showNumber){
        var floorContent = thisfloor.find('.gfloorContent');
        var header = thisfloor.find('.gfloorHeader');
        var losswidth = maxWdith - screenwidth;
        var perlosswidth = losswidth / showNumber;
        var firstline = thisfloor.find('.gfloor-first-line');
        var secondline = thisfloor.find('.gfloor-second-line');
        hidecell(firstline,showNumber);
        hidecell(secondline,showNumber);
        var allwidth = 210*showNumber-losswidth
        floorContent.width(allwidth);
        header.width(allwidth);
        thisfloor.find('.gfloorfbrand').css({'margin-top':30-perlosswidth/3});
        thisfloor.find('.gfloorsbrand').css({'margin-top':30-perlosswidth/3});
        firstline.width(allwidth+1);firstline.height(210-perlosswidth);
        secondline.width(allwidth+1);secondline.height(210-perlosswidth);
        thisfloor.find('.gfloorcell').width(210-perlosswidth);
        thisfloor.find('.gfloorcell').height(210-perlosswidth);
        thisfloor.find('.gfloorbigprice').css({'font-size':42-perlosswidth/3});
        thisfloor.find('.gfnewContent').css({'font-size':24-perlosswidth/10});
        thisfloor.find('.gfcontentbuy').css({'bottom':40-perlosswidth/3});
    }
    function hideType(fline, lossNum, typename){
        var hideCell = fline.find(typename);
        var hideSize = hideCell.length;
        if (lossNum>0){
            for (var i=hideSize-1;i>=0;i--){
                hideCell[i].style.display='none';
                lossNum--;
                if (lossNum<=0){
                    for (var j=i-1;j>=0;j--)
                        hideCell[j].style.display='block';
                    break;
                }
            }
        } else {
            for (var j=0;j<hideSize;j++)
                hideCell[j].style.display='block';
        }
        return lossNum;
    }
    function hidecell(fline,showNumber){
        var lossNumber = 7-showNumber;
        lossNumber = hideType(fline,lossNumber, '.gfloorhotword');
        lossNumber = hideType(fline,lossNumber, '.gfloorasinbs');
        
        var promotionCell = fline.find('.gfloorpromotiontext');
        var asinCell = fline.find('.gfloorasincell');
        var promotionSize = promotionCell.length;
        var asinSize = asinCell.length;
        
        if (lossNumber>0){
            var lossPACell = asinSize*2-(showNumber-1);
            if (lossPACell<0)
                lossPACell = 0;
            var lossPair = Math.floor(lossPACell/2);
            for (var i=0;i<lossPair;i++){
                promotionCell[promotionSize-i-1] && promotionCell[promotionSize-i-1].style && (promotionCell[promotionSize-i-1].style.display = 'none');
                asinCell[asinSize-i-1] && asinCell[asinSize-i-1].style && (asinCell[asinSize-i-1].style.display = 'none');
            }
            if (lossPACell%2==1){
                asinCell[asinSize-lossPair-1] && asinCell[asinSize-lossPair-1].style && (asinCell[asinSize-lossPair-1].style.display='none');
                promotionCell[asinSize-lossPair-1] && promotionCell[asinSize-lossPair-1].style && (promotionCell[asinSize-lossPair-1].style.display='block');
            } else {
                asinCell[asinSize-lossPair-1] && asinCell[asinSize-lossPair-1].style && (asinCell[asinSize-lossPair-1].style.display='block');
                promotionCell[asinSize-lossPair-1] && promotionCell[asinSize-lossPair-1].style && (promotionCell[asinSize-lossPair-1].style.display='block');
            }
            for (var i=0;i<asinSize-lossPair-1;i++){
                asinCell[i] && asinCell[i].style && (asinCell[i].style.display='block');
                promotionCell[i] && promotionCell[i].style && (promotionCell[i].style.display='block');
            }
        } else {
            for (var j=0;j<asinSize;j++){
                asinCell[j] && asinCell[j].style && (asinCell[j].style.display='block');
                promotionCell[j] && promotionCell[j].style && (promotionCell[j].style.display='block');
            }
        }
        
        
    }
}
function BMVDRender($){
    $.ajax({
        type: 'POST',
        url: '/gp/grid-floor-widget/ajaxGetGridContent.html/462-8128257-5838428',
        data: {"floorType":"BMVD","rId":"52JX2PQC4DK5BPD5MQ43","arrow":"https://images-cn.ssl-images-amazon.com/images/G/28/gwfloor/static/images/arrow_small_white._CB304609528_.png","redirectUrl":"#?pf_rd_p=0099ad5c-dcea-40c9-b478-0521b0a010a9&pf_rd_s=desktop-8&pf_rd_t=36701&pf_rd_i=desktop&pf_rd_m=A1AJ19PSB66TGU&pf_rd_r=52JX2PQC4DK5BPD5MQ43&pf_rd_r=52JX2PQC4DK5BPD5MQ43&pf_rd_p=0099ad5c-dcea-40c9-b478-0521b0a010a9"},
        dataType: 'text',
        cache: false,
        contentType: 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded; charset=utf-8',
        timeout: 40000,
        success: function(data) {
            data = eval('('+data+')');
            var contentHtml = data.contentHtml;
            $('#BMVDgfloorcontent').append(contentHtml);
            $('#BMVDgfloorcontent .gfloorasincelldiv').css({'opacity':0.85});
            $('#BMVDgfloorcontent .gfloorblockcell').css({'opacity':0.8});
            $('#BMVDgfloorcontent .gfloorasincelldiv').hover(
                function(){
                    $(this).stop(true,true).animate({opacity:0.95},200);
                },
                function(){
                    $(this).stop(true,true).animate({opacity:0.85},200);
                }
            );
            $('#BMVDgfloorcontent .gfloorblockcell').hover(
                function(){
                    $(this).stop(true,true).animate({opacity:0.9},200);
                },
                function(){
                    $(this).stop(true,true).animate({opacity:0.8},200);
                }
            );
            $('#BMVDgfloorcontent .gfloorpromotiontext').hover(
                function(){
                    $(this).find('.gfcontentbspan').css({'color':'#E47911'});
                },
                function(){
                    $(this).find('.gfcontentbspan').css({'color':'#767676'});
                }
            );
            $('#BMVDgfloorcontent .gfloorbstext').hover(
                function(){
                    $(this).find('.gfcontentbspan').css({'color':'#E47911'});
                },
                function(){
                    $(this).find('.gfcontentbspan').css({'color':'#767676'});
                }
            );
            BMVDresize($, $('#BMVDgfloor'),1);
        }
    });
}
if (typeof amznJQ !== 'undefined'){
    amznJQ.available('jQuery',function(){
        var $ = jQuery;
        var thisfloor = $('#BMVDgfloor');
        BMVDcheck($);
        $(window).scroll(function(){
            if (BMVDgfloorstatus == 0){
                BMVDcheck($);
            }
        });
    });
} else if (typeof P !== 'undefined'){
    P.when('A').execute(function(A){
        var $ = A.$;
        var thisfloor = $('#BMVDgfloor');
        BMVDcheck($);
        $(window).scroll(function(){
            if (BMVDgfloorstatus == 0){
                BMVDcheck($);
            }
        });
    });
}
</script>

class="gfloortitlecontent"><span>&#x5c45;&#x5bb6;&#x751f;&#x6d3b;&#x9986;</span></div></div><div class="gfloorHeaderSplit"></div><div class="gfloorHeaderLinks"><ul><li><a <script type="text/javascript">
var HARDLINEgfloorstatus = 0;
function HARDLINEcheck($){
    var windowtop  = $(window).scrollTop();
    var windowfoot = windowtop+$(window).height();
    var preheight  = 400;
    var thisfloor  = $('#HARDLINEgfloor');
    var floorheight= 470;
    var floortop   = thisfloor.offset().top;
    var floorfoot  = floortop+floorheight;
    if ((floortop>windowfoot && floortop<windowfoot+preheight) 
        || (floorfoot<windowtop && floorfoot+preheight>windowtop) 
        || (floorfoot>windowtop && floortop<windowfoot)){
            HARDLINEgfloorstatus = 1;
            HARDLINERender($);
            $(window).resize(function(){
                HARDLINEresize($, thisfloor,0);
            });
    }
}
function HARDLINEresize($,thisfloor,status){
    var screenwidth = thisfloor.width();
    if (screenwidth>=1470){
        alterfloor(7);
    } else if (screenwidth<1470 && screenwidth>=1260){
        changesize(1470,7);
    } else if (screenwidth<1260 && screenwidth>=1080) {
        changesize(1260,6);
    } else if (screenwidth<1080 && screenwidth>=1040) {
        alterfloor(5);
    } else if (screenwidth<1040 && screenwidth>=900) {
        changesize(1040,5);
    } else if (screenwidth<900 && screenwidth>=840) {
        alterfloor(4);
    } else if (screenwidth<840 && screenwidth>=720) {
        changesize(840,4);
    } else if (screenwidth<720) {
        alterfloor(3);
    }
    function alterfloor(showNumber){
        var floorContent = thisfloor.find('.gfloorContent');
        var header = thisfloor.find('.gfloorHeader');
        var firstline = thisfloor.find('.gfloor-first-line');
        var secondline = thisfloor.find('.gfloor-second-line');
        hidecell(firstline,showNumber);
        hidecell(secondline,showNumber);
        floorContent.width(210*showNumber);
        header.width(210*showNumber);
        thisfloor.find('.gfloorfbrand').css({'margin-top':30});
        thisfloor.find('.gfloorsbrand').css({'margin-top':30});
        firstline.width(210*showNumber);firstline.height(210);
        secondline.width(210*showNumber);secondline.height(210);
        thisfloor.find('.gfloorcell').width(210);
        thisfloor.find('.gfloorcell').height(210);
        thisfloor.find('.gfloorbigprice').css({'font-size':42});
        thisfloor.find('.gfnewContent').css({'font-size':24});
        thisfloor.find('.gfcontentbuy').css({'bottom':40});
    }
    
    function changesize(maxWdith,showNumber){
        var floorContent = thisfloor.find('.gfloorContent');
        var header = thisfloor.find('.gfloorHeader');
        var losswidth = maxWdith - screenwidth;
        var perlosswidth = losswidth / showNumber;
        var firstline = thisfloor.find('.gfloor-first-line');
        var secondline = thisfloor.find('.gfloor-second-line');
        hidecell(firstline,showNumber);
        hidecell(secondline,showNumber);
        var allwidth = 210*showNumber-losswidth
        floorContent.width(allwidth);
        header.width(allwidth);
        thisfloor.find('.gfloorfbrand').css({'margin-top':30-perlosswidth/3});
        thisfloor.find('.gfloorsbrand').css({'margin-top':30-perlosswidth/3});
        firstline.width(allwidth+1);firstline.height(210-perlosswidth);
        secondline.width(allwidth+1);secondline.height(210-perlosswidth);
        thisfloor.find('.gfloorcell').width(210-perlosswidth);
        thisfloor.find('.gfloorcell').height(210-perlosswidth);
        thisfloor.find('.gfloorbigprice').css({'font-size':42-perlosswidth/3});
        thisfloor.find('.gfnewContent').css({'font-size':24-perlosswidth/10});
        thisfloor.find('.gfcontentbuy').css({'bottom':40-perlosswidth/3});
    }
    function hideType(fline, lossNum, typename){
        var hideCell = fline.find(typename);
        var hideSize = hideCell.length;
        if (lossNum>0){
            for (var i=hideSize-1;i>=0;i--){
                hideCell[i].style.display='none';
                lossNum--;
                if (lossNum<=0){
                    for (var j=i-1;j>=0;j--)
                        hideCell[j].style.display='block';
                    break;
                }
            }
        } else {
            for (var j=0;j<hideSize;j++)
                hideCell[j].style.display='block';
        }
        return lossNum;
    }
    function hidecell(fline,showNumber){
        var lossNumber = 7-showNumber;
        lossNumber = hideType(fline,lossNumber, '.gfloorhotword');
        lossNumber = hideType(fline,lossNumber, '.gfloorasinbs');
        
        var promotionCell = fline.find('.gfloorpromotiontext');
        var asinCell = fline.find('.gfloorasincell');
        var promotionSize = promotionCell.length;
        var asinSize = asinCell.length;
        
        if (lossNumber>0){
            var lossPACell = asinSize*2-(showNumber-1);
            if (lossPACell<0)
                lossPACell = 0;
            var lossPair = Math.floor(lossPACell/2);
            for (var i=0;i<lossPair;i++){
                promotionCell[promotionSize-i-1] && promotionCell[promotionSize-i-1].style && (promotionCell[promotionSize-i-1].style.display = 'none');
                asinCell[asinSize-i-1] && asinCell[asinSize-i-1].style && (asinCell[asinSize-i-1].style.display = 'none');
            }
            if (lossPACell%2==1){
                asinCell[asinSize-lossPair-1] && asinCell[asinSize-lossPair-1].style && (asinCell[asinSize-lossPair-1].style.display='none');
                promotionCell[asinSize-lossPair-1] && promotionCell[asinSize-lossPair-1].style && (promotionCell[asinSize-lossPair-1].style.display='block');
            } else {
                asinCell[asinSize-lossPair-1] && asinCell[asinSize-lossPair-1].style && (asinCell[asinSize-lossPair-1].style.display='block');
                promotionCell[asinSize-lossPair-1] && promotionCell[asinSize-lossPair-1].style && (promotionCell[asinSize-lossPair-1].style.display='block');
            }
            for (var i=0;i<asinSize-lossPair-1;i++){
                asinCell[i] && asinCell[i].style && (asinCell[i].style.display='block');
                promotionCell[i] && promotionCell[i].style && (promotionCell[i].style.display='block');
            }
        } else {
            for (var j=0;j<asinSize;j++){
                asinCell[j] && asinCell[j].style && (asinCell[j].style.display='block');
                promotionCell[j] && promotionCell[j].style && (promotionCell[j].style.display='block');
            }
        }
        
        
    }
}
function HARDLINERender($){
    $.ajax({
        type: 'POST',
        url: '/gp/grid-floor-widget/ajaxGetGridContent.html/462-8128257-5838428',
        data: {"floorType":"HARDLINE","rId":"52JX2PQC4DK5BPD5MQ43","arrow":"https://images-cn.ssl-images-amazon.com/images/G/28/gwfloor/static/images/arrow_small_white._CB304609528_.png","redirectUrl":"#?pf_rd_p=dd685159-82d5-4f9d-a942-96ecf4e3e9bb&pf_rd_s=desktop-10&pf_rd_t=36701&pf_rd_i=desktop&pf_rd_m=A1AJ19PSB66TGU&pf_rd_r=52JX2PQC4DK5BPD5MQ43&pf_rd_r=52JX2PQC4DK5BPD5MQ43&pf_rd_p=dd685159-82d5-4f9d-a942-96ecf4e3e9bb"},
        dataType: 'text',
        cache: false,
        contentType: 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded; charset=utf-8',
        timeout: 40000,
        success: function(data) {
            data = eval('('+data+')');
            var contentHtml = data.contentHtml;
            $('#HARDLINEgfloorcontent').append(contentHtml);
            $('#HARDLINEgfloorcontent .gfloorasincelldiv').css({'opacity':0.85});
            $('#HARDLINEgfloorcontent .gfloorblockcell').css({'opacity':0.8});
            $('#HARDLINEgfloorcontent .gfloorasincelldiv').hover(
                function(){
                    $(this).stop(true,true).animate({opacity:0.95},200);
                },
                function(){
                    $(this).stop(true,true).animate({opacity:0.85},200);
                }
            );
            $('#HARDLINEgfloorcontent .gfloorblockcell').hover(
                function(){
                    $(this).stop(true,true).animate({opacity:0.9},200);
                },
                function(){
                    $(this).stop(true,true).animate({opacity:0.8},200);
                }
            );
            $('#HARDLINEgfloorcontent .gfloorpromotiontext').hover(
                function(){
                    $(this).find('.gfcontentbspan').css({'color':'#E47911'});
                },
                function(){
                    $(this).find('.gfcontentbspan').css({'color':'#767676'});
                }
            );
            $('#HARDLINEgfloorcontent .gfloorbstext').hover(
                function(){
                    $(this).find('.gfcontentbspan').css({'color':'#E47911'});
                },
                function(){
                    $(this).find('.gfcontentbspan').css({'color':'#767676'});
                }
            );
            HARDLINEresize($, $('#HARDLINEgfloor'),1);
        }
    });
}
if (typeof amznJQ !== 'undefined'){
    amznJQ.available('jQuery',function(){
        var $ = jQuery;
        var thisfloor = $('#HARDLINEgfloor');
        HARDLINEcheck($);
        $(window).scroll(function(){
            if (HARDLINEgfloorstatus == 0){
                HARDLINEcheck($);
            }
        });
    });
} else if (typeof P !== 'undefined'){
    P.when('A').execute(function(A){
        var $ = A.$;
        var thisfloor = $('#HARDLINEgfloor');
        HARDLINEcheck($);
        $(window).scroll(function(){
            if (HARDLINEgfloorstatus == 0){
                HARDLINEcheck($);
            }
        });
    });
}
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
var CONSUMABLEgfloorstatus = 0;
function CONSUMABLEcheck($){
    var windowtop  = $(window).scrollTop();
    var windowfoot = windowtop+$(window).height();
    var preheight  = 400;
    var thisfloor  = $('#CONSUMABLEgfloor');
    var floorheight= 470;
    var floortop   = thisfloor.offset().top;
    var floorfoot  = floortop+floorheight;
    if ((floortop>windowfoot && floortop<windowfoot+preheight) 
        || (floorfoot<windowtop && floorfoot+preheight>windowtop) 
        || (floorfoot>windowtop && floortop<windowfoot)){
            CONSUMABLEgfloorstatus = 1;
            CONSUMABLERender($);
            $(window).resize(function(){
                CONSUMABLEresize($, thisfloor,0);
            });
    }
}
function CONSUMABLEresize($,thisfloor,status){
    var screenwidth = thisfloor.width();
    if (screenwidth>=1470){
        alterfloor(7);
    } else if (screenwidth<1470 && screenwidth>=1260){
        changesize(1470,7);
    } else if (screenwidth<1260 && screenwidth>=1080) {
        changesize(1260,6);
    } else if (screenwidth<1080 && screenwidth>=1040) {
        alterfloor(5);
    } else if (screenwidth<1040 && screenwidth>=900) {
        changesize(1040,5);
    } else if (screenwidth<900 && screenwidth>=840) {
        alterfloor(4);
    } else if (screenwidth<840 && screenwidth>=720) {
        changesize(840,4);
    } else if (screenwidth<720) {
        alterfloor(3);
    }
    function alterfloor(showNumber){
        var floorContent = thisfloor.find('.gfloorContent');
        var header = thisfloor.find('.gfloorHeader');
        var firstline = thisfloor.find('.gfloor-first-line');
        var secondline = thisfloor.find('.gfloor-second-line');
        hidecell(firstline,showNumber);
        hidecell(secondline,showNumber);
        floorContent.width(210*showNumber);
        header.width(210*showNumber);
        thisfloor.find('.gfloorfbrand').css({'margin-top':30});
        thisfloor.find('.gfloorsbrand').css({'margin-top':30});
        firstline.width(210*showNumber);firstline.height(210);
        secondline.width(210*showNumber);secondline.height(210);
        thisfloor.find('.gfloorcell').width(210);
        thisfloor.find('.gfloorcell').height(210);
        thisfloor.find('.gfloorbigprice').css({'font-size':42});
        thisfloor.find('.gfnewContent').css({'font-size':24});
        thisfloor.find('.gfcontentbuy').css({'bottom':40});
    }
    
    function changesize(maxWdith,showNumber){
        var floorContent = thisfloor.find('.gfloorContent');
        var header = thisfloor.find('.gfloorHeader');
        var losswidth = maxWdith - screenwidth;
        var perlosswidth = losswidth / showNumber;
        var firstline = thisfloor.find('.gfloor-first-line');
        var secondline = thisfloor.find('.gfloor-second-line');
        hidecell(firstline,showNumber);
        hidecell(secondline,showNumber);
        var allwidth = 210*showNumber-losswidth
        floorContent.width(allwidth);
        header.width(allwidth);
        thisfloor.find('.gfloorfbrand').css({'margin-top':30-perlosswidth/3});
        thisfloor.find('.gfloorsbrand').css({'margin-top':30-perlosswidth/3});
        firstline.width(allwidth+1);firstline.height(210-perlosswidth);
        secondline.width(allwidth+1);secondline.height(210-perlosswidth);
        thisfloor.find('.gfloorcell').width(210-perlosswidth);
        thisfloor.find('.gfloorcell').height(210-perlosswidth);
        thisfloor.find('.gfloorbigprice').css({'font-size':42-perlosswidth/3});
        thisfloor.find('.gfnewContent').css({'font-size':24-perlosswidth/10});
        thisfloor.find('.gfcontentbuy').css({'bottom':40-perlosswidth/3});
    }
    function hideType(fline, lossNum, typename){
        var hideCell = fline.find(typename);
        var hideSize = hideCell.length;
        if (lossNum>0){
            for (var i=hideSize-1;i>=0;i--){
                hideCell[i].style.display='none';
                lossNum--;
                if (lossNum<=0){
                    for (var j=i-1;j>=0;j--)
                        hideCell[j].style.display='block';
                    break;
                }
            }
        } else {
            for (var j=0;j<hideSize;j++)
                hideCell[j].style.display='block';
        }
        return lossNum;
    }
    function hidecell(fline,showNumber){
        var lossNumber = 7-showNumber;
        lossNumber = hideType(fline,lossNumber, '.gfloorhotword');
        lossNumber = hideType(fline,lossNumber, '.gfloorasinbs');
        
        var promotionCell = fline.find('.gfloorpromotiontext');
        var asinCell = fline.find('.gfloorasincell');
        var promotionSize = promotionCell.length;
        var asinSize = asinCell.length;
        
        if (lossNumber>0){
            var lossPACell = asinSize*2-(showNumber-1);
            if (lossPACell<0)
                lossPACell = 0;
            var lossPair = Math.floor(lossPACell/2);
            for (var i=0;i<lossPair;i++){
                promotionCell[promotionSize-i-1] && promotionCell[promotionSize-i-1].style && (promotionCell[promotionSize-i-1].style.display = 'none');
                asinCell[asinSize-i-1] && asinCell[asinSize-i-1].style && (asinCell[asinSize-i-1].style.display = 'none');
            }
            if (lossPACell%2==1){
                asinCell[asinSize-lossPair-1] && asinCell[asinSize-lossPair-1].style && (asinCell[asinSize-lossPair-1].style.display='none');
                promotionCell[asinSize-lossPair-1] && promotionCell[asinSize-lossPair-1].style && (promotionCell[asinSize-lossPair-1].style.display='block');
            } else {
                asinCell[asinSize-lossPair-1] && asinCell[asinSize-lossPair-1].style && (asinCell[asinSize-lossPair-1].style.display='block');
                promotionCell[asinSize-lossPair-1] && promotionCell[asinSize-lossPair-1].style && (promotionCell[asinSize-lossPair-1].style.display='block');
            }
            for (var i=0;i<asinSize-lossPair-1;i++){
                asinCell[i] && asinCell[i].style && (asinCell[i].style.display='block');
                promotionCell[i] && promotionCell[i].style && (promotionCell[i].style.display='block');
            }
        } else {
            for (var j=0;j<asinSize;j++){
                asinCell[j] && asinCell[j].style && (asinCell[j].style.display='block');
                promotionCell[j] && promotionCell[j].style && (promotionCell[j].style.display='block');
            }
        }
        
        
    }
}
function CONSUMABLERender($){
    $.ajax({
        type: 'POST',
        url: '/gp/grid-floor-widget/ajaxGetGridContent.html/462-8128257-5838428',
        data: {"floorType":"CONSUMABLE","rId":"52JX2PQC4DK5BPD5MQ43","arrow":"https://images-cn.ssl-images-amazon.com/images/G/28/gwfloor/static/images/arrow_small_white._CB304609528_.png","redirectUrl":"#?pf_rd_p=f845a2d0-fe5a-42ad-8b0a-422fc820265a&pf_rd_s=desktop-11&pf_rd_t=36701&pf_rd_i=desktop&pf_rd_m=A1AJ19PSB66TGU&pf_rd_r=52JX2PQC4DK5BPD5MQ43&pf_rd_r=52JX2PQC4DK5BPD5MQ43&pf_rd_p=f845a2d0-fe5a-42ad-8b0a-422fc820265a"},
        dataType: 'text',
        cache: false,
        contentType: 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded; charset=utf-8',
        timeout: 40000,
        success: function(data) {
            data = eval('('+data+')');
            var contentHtml = data.contentHtml;
            $('#CONSUMABLEgfloorcontent').append(contentHtml);
            $('#CONSUMABLEgfloorcontent .gfloorasincelldiv').css({'opacity':0.85});
            $('#CONSUMABLEgfloorcontent .gfloorblockcell').css({'opacity':0.8});
            $('#CONSUMABLEgfloorcontent .gfloorasincelldiv').hover(
                function(){
                    $(this).stop(true,true).animate({opacity:0.95},200);
                },
                function(){
                    $(this).stop(true,true).animate({opacity:0.85},200);
                }
            );
            $('#CONSUMABLEgfloorcontent .gfloorblockcell').hover(
                function(){
                    $(this).stop(true,true).animate({opacity:0.9},200);
                },
                function(){
                    $(this).stop(true,true).animate({opacity:0.8},200);
                }
            );
            $('#CONSUMABLEgfloorcontent .gfloorpromotiontext').hover(
                function(){
                    $(this).find('.gfcontentbspan').css({'color':'#E47911'});
                },
                function(){
                    $(this).find('.gfcontentbspan').css({'color':'#767676'});
                }
            );
            $('#CONSUMABLEgfloorcontent .gfloorbstext').hover(
                function(){
                    $(this).find('.gfcontentbspan').css({'color':'#E47911'});
                },
                function(){
                    $(this).find('.gfcontentbspan').css({'color':'#767676'});
                }
            );
            CONSUMABLEresize($, $('#CONSUMABLEgfloor'),1);
        }
    });
}
if (typeof amznJQ !== 'undefined'){
    amznJQ.available('jQuery',function(){
        var $ = jQuery;
        var thisfloor = $('#CONSUMABLEgfloor');
        CONSUMABLEcheck($);
        $(window).scroll(function(){
            if (CONSUMABLEgfloorstatus == 0){
                CONSUMABLEcheck($);
            }
        });
    });
} else if (typeof P !== 'undefined'){
    P.when('A').execute(function(A){
        var $ = A.$;
        var thisfloor = $('#CONSUMABLEgfloor');
        CONSUMABLEcheck($);
        $(window).scroll(function(){
            if (CONSUMABLEgfloorstatus == 0){
                CONSUMABLEcheck($);
            }
        });
    });
}

            if (lossPACell<0)
                lossPACell = 0;
            var lossPair = Math.floor(lossPACell/2);
            for (var i=0;i<lossPair;i++){
                promotionCell[promotionSize-i-1] && promotionCell[promotionSize-i-1].style && (promotionCell[promotionSize-i-1].style.display = 'none');
                asinCell[asinSize-i-1] && asinCell[asinSize-i-1].style && (asinCell[asinSize-i-1].style.display = 'none');
            }
            if (lossPACell%2==1){
                asinCell[asinSize-lossPair-1] && asinCell[asinSize-lossPair-1].style && (asinCell[asinSize-lossPair-1].style.display='none');
                promotionCell[asinSize-lossPair-1] && promotionCell[asinSize-lossPair-1].style && (promotionCell[asinSize-lossPair-1].style.display='block');
            } else {
                asinCell[asinSize-lossPair-1] && asinCell[asinSize-lossPair-1].style && (asinCell[asinSize-lossPair-1].style.display='block');
                promotionCell[asinSize-lossPair-1] && promotionCell[asinSize-lossPair-1].style && (promotionCell[asinSize-lossPair-1].style.display='block');
            }
            for (var i=0;i<asinSize-lossPair-1;i++){
                asinCell[i] && asinCell[i].style && (asinCell[i].style.display='block');
                promotionCell[i] && promotionCell[i].style && (promotionCell[i].style.display='block');
            }
        } else {
            for (var j=0;j<asinSize;j++){
                asinCell[j] && asinCell[j].style && (asinCell[j].style.display='block');
                promotionCell[j] && promotionCell[j].style && (promotionCell[j].style.display='block');
            }
        }
        
        
    }
}
